# 2.2 DlData

## 2.2.1 General DlData

**2.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11512275`)

General DlData
Description: DL data transfer

Used by: 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO

Addressing: 5G\_L1\_IF\_14416

---

DlData Interface Principles
[Before CNI-98319]

For Loki-L1-HW [RP003187-E] and Thor [End RP003187-E], 5G-L1-DL shall use information from msgCountCtrl IE from arriving DlData\_\*SendReq messages to trigger datapath processing before end of the reception window (value B) specified under 5G\_L1\_IF\_121\_replaced([11513225](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTl_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before PR591229] Before 5G21B

msgCountCtrl IE contains following information:

* lastMsg (1 bit, boolean): True for the last DlData\_\*SendReq sent by the 5G-L2-PS (UL or DL) scheduler for a given subcell/slot; False for other requests.
* lastMsgCount (3 bits): number of messages with lastMsg set to True in a given subcell/slot. Depends on the number of active schedulers in a given subcell/slot.
* msgCount (4 bits): valid only when lastMsg is True. Contains total count of DlData\_\*SendReq messages that were scheduled by the UL or DL scheduler for a given subcell/slot (DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is not counted).

[End PR591229]

[PR591229]  5G21B and onwards

msgCountCtrl IE contains following information:

* lastMsg (1 bit, boolean): True for the last DlData\_\*SendReq sent by the 5G-L2-PS (UL or DL) scheduler for a given subcell/slot; False for other requests.
* lastMsgCount (2 bits): number of messages with lastMsg set to True in a given subcell/slot. Depends on the number of active schedulers in a given subcell/slot.
* msgCount (5 bits): valid only when lastMsg is True. Contains total count of DlData\_\*SendReq messages that were scheduled by the UL or DL scheduler for a given subcell/slot (DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, DlData\_SlotTypeReq and DlData\_PatternConfigReq are not counted).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating a data structure divided into several segments, labeled with text and color-coded. The structure is oriented horizontally, with "MSB" (Most Significant Bit) indicated on the left and "LSB" (Least Significant Bit) on the right.
The top row consists of colored rectangular segments. The leftmost segment is a dark blue, followed by two lighter blue segments, and then four segments of the lightest blue.
The bottom row contains text labels corresponding to these segments. From left to right, the labels are: "lastMsg", "lastMsgCount", and "msgCount". The "lastMsg" label is positioned under the dark blue segment. The "lastMsgCount" label is under the first two lighter blue segments. The "msgCount" label spans across the remaining four lightest blue segments.
The overall structure suggests a representation of data fields within a message or packet, where "lastMsg" and "lastMsgCount" are distinct fields, and "msgCount" is a larger field. The color gradient likely indicates the relative size or importance of these fields, with darker colors representing smaller or more significant parts.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_47.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[End PR591229]

Upon receiving DlData\_\*SendReq message, 5G-L1-DL shall:

- Count messages with lastMsg = True up to lastMsgCount.

5G-L1-DL can assume that lastMsgCount is the same across all received messages in a given subcell/slot.

- Count messages up to Y, where Y is the sum of msgCount over all messages with lastMsg = True.

- If number of received messages is equal to Y, then 5G-L1-DL shall trigger datapath processing.

Note:

* If there is no DL channel/signal to be sent for a subcell/slot from DL or UL scheduler(s), 5G-L2-PS sends DlData\_EmptySendReq message with msgCountCtrl IE filled as follows:
* lastMsg = True
* lastMsgCount = the number of active schedulers in this subcell/slot
* msgCount = 1
* If DlData\_EmptySendReq acts as a replacement message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_105\_replaced([11513105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFgvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then msgCountCtrl IE in this message is filled as follows:
* lastMsg = True
* lastMsgCount set as in other messages
* msgCount = number of DL channel/signal sent from DL or UL scheduler including DlData\_EmptySendReq.
* DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, DlData\_SlotTypeReq and DlData\_PatternConfigReq shall not be counted.

[CNI-98319]

msgCountCtrl IE is removed from DlData\_\*SendReq messages.

[End CNI-98319]

---

## 2.2.3 NR-slot Type Configuration

**2.2.3.0-10**  (ID: `11512413`)

NR-slot Type Configuration
**DlData\_SlotTypeReq message content:**

The slotType is no more used by the L1 on CPRI configuration since 19B.

Since 19B and on eCPRI configurations, the slotType is no more used by the L1 except for the PRACH slots and when the actEcpriPhase2 is set to false, for the SS/PBCH slots.

When the slot type is not used, the L1 relies on the regular messages sent by the L2 (DlData\_SsBlockSendReq, DlData\_CsiRsSendReq...).

**[PR531473] 5G20 and onwards**

**For Graceful Cell Shutdown, L2 need send the request in slot contain SSB,** L1 check pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB field but not slotType filed in the message. this is common for CPRI and e-CPRI\*\*\*\*

**[End PR531473]**

**[CNI-81900]L2-PS only sends SlotTypeReq if it has non-zero powerReduction value for at least one symbol in the slot. No more slot types communication between L2-PS and L1-SW.**[End CNI-81900]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009027-5G-A] 5G-L1-DL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support the requirements of CNI-81900 in Thor**. [End CB009027-5G-A]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-A] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End RP003187-A]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-H] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End RP003187-H]\*\*\*\*

**[Before CNI-122313]**

**[CB009858-C, CB009443] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in RINLINE 1.**[End CB009858-C, CB009443]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2** [End CNI-122313]\*\*\*\*

**[CB008313-B] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in Loki**[End CB008313-B]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009851-F] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in RINLINE2 for TDD eCPRI.**[End CB009851-F]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007814-A] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in Loki.**[End CB007814-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007271-C] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in Loki for FDD-CPRI.**[End CB007271-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB008423-A] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above in Loki TDD CPRI.**[End CB008423-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007539-B] 5G-L1-DL shall also support the requirements above.**[End CB007539-B]\*\*\*\*

**NOTE: Starting from 5G20B onwards, there is no need to define new slot types. The IE slotType shall be filled properly for PRACH (set to 0 for PRACH see below) and when the actEcpriPhase2 is set to false, for SSB slots (2 for SSB, see below). Otherwise this IE is useless** and can be set to any value in the right range.\*\*\*\*

| slotType                | u8 [0..127]            | 0: PRACH (slot which carries PRACH but potentially also PDCCH and PUCCH 1: Not used 2: SSBURST (slot which carries SS blocks with PSS, SSS & PBCH, CSI-RS; potentially also carries PDCCH, PUCCH - to be confirmed). More details about the supported configurations of the SSB slots are in 5G\_L1\_IF\_521\_replaced([11516432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSEDsfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).   Ul & Dl Data NR-slots defined in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_10271. 20: Dl data NR-slot C2\_TX (not used) 21: Ul data NR-slot C2 22: Dl data NR-slot B1 23: Not used 24: Not used 25: Not used   NOTE: B1\_CSC and C2\_CSC are supported only for ABIK.   Additionally supported slot types are in 5G\_L1\_IF\_50\_replaced([11512386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRpM8_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).   5GC001037-A/E: u8 [0..51], u8 [0..55]   5GC001258-A: u8 [0..62]   **[PR627923]: u8 [0..127] [End PR627923]**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 [0...127]                                 | 5GC001037-A 5GC001037-E 5GC001258-A |
| pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB | array[14] of u8        | For all the NR-slots except the one(s) carrying the SS burst pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB[n] is applied to an OFDM symbol n of the NR-slot.   Power reduction per RE compared to the DL power computed from parameters coming from DlData\_PdschSendReq (i.e. pdschTbTransmitPower)): 0 for normal behavior (no power reduction). [1..50] are for the power reduction applied to the channel transmit power with a step of 1dB (that is, real transmit power = channel transmit power - pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB). Values [51 ..255] can be used to mute the symbol.   For the NR-slots carrying SS burst below 6GHz: pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB[n] is applied to an OFDM symbol n of the NR-slot For the NR-slots carrying SS burst above 6GHz: pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB[n] is applied to scs 120 kHz OFDM symbol n of the NR-slot pair or scs 240 kHz OFDM symbol pair 2*n & 2*n+1 of the NR-slot pair.   Power reduction per RE compared to the DL power computed from parameters coming from DlCell\_SetupReq (i.e. ssBlockPower): 0 for normal behavior (no power reduction). [1..50] are for the power reduction applied to the channel transmit power with a step of 1dB (that is, for each symbol of the SS block: real transmit power = channel transmit power - pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB). Values [51 ..255] can be used to mute the symbol. Note: this power reduction does not apply to CSI-RS REs as it is handled in DlData\_CsiRsSendReq message.   Note: above 6GHz, SS burst up to the tester to identify the 2 adjacent indexes in order to identify the right SS block (index m for OFDM symbols (PSS+PBCH) & index m+1 for OFDM symbols (SSS+PBCH)) see 5G-L1\_IF\_5145.   [5GC000501-A] Parameter pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB is also used for Graceful Cell Shutdown mechanism by increasing the value by 3dB at each power reduction step for all OFDM symbols carrying Synchronization Signals. More details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2584 [End 5GC000501-A] | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** array[14] of u8                              | 5GC000501-A                         |

## 2.2.4 5G RF Pattern Configuration

**2.2.4.0-8**  (ID: `11512461`)

5G RF Pattern Configuration
**DlData\_PatternConfigReq message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **Client** Reference\*\*\*\* | **L1 HW Support** | **First Feature** |
| subcellId | u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gvuZ8WGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). SubcellId is meant to be used as unrestricted ID and therefore L1 should accept any u8(exclude 0xFF) value. | 5G\_UP\_1851 | Loner: u8 [0...7] **Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | 5GC001626-B |
| sfn | u16 [0..1023] | System Frame Number (38.211 §4.3.1 & 38.331 §6.2.2) |  | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u16 [0..1023] |  |
| slot | u8 [0..79] | NR-slot (38.211 §4.3.2) |  | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 [0..79] |  |
| txRxBitmapPol | u16 | Bitmap (14 bits) that indicates the direction of symbols. The first bit at position 0 indicates Tx/Rx of the first symbol and bit at position 13 indicates Tx/Rx for the last symbol.   For RACH Format 0 12 bits For RACH Format 1 10 bits See parameter numOfPatterIdPol for clarification. For each bit, 1 means Tx, 0 means Rx or GP. | 5G\_L2\_486 | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u16 |  |
| numOfPatternIdPol | u8 | Number of control blocks for each polarization. The patterns are listed in the order of increasing symbol numbers in the NR-slot. The value is set to 14 indicating one control block per symbol in the NR-slot for all type of NR-slot but PRACH.   For PRACH (see 5G\_L1\_3853\_replaced([11494713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEo71PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the PRACH format), the value is set to 14 with one control vector per symbol. | 5G\_L2\_486 | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 |  |
| numOfXpolBeams | {1,2,4} | Number of valid XpolBeam(cross-polarized beam) in patternIdPolList   **[5GC002249-D] in ECPRI, in case of actEcpriPhase2 activated (5G\_L1\_IF\_20\_replaced([11512165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRnXwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_IF\_158\_replaced([11513484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this IE is not valid and shall not be read.** [End 5GC002249-D]\*\*\*\* | 5G\_L2\_871 | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** {1,2,4} | 5GC001626-B 5GC002249-D |
| bfcmOffset | u8 [0…31] | Control vector offset in BFCM message where DFE vector list from patternIdPolList shall be copied to BFCM message for each control block (symbol). **[5GC002249-D] in ECPRI, in case of actEcpriPhase2 activated (5G\_L1\_IF\_20\_replaced([11512165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRnXwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_IF\_158\_replaced([11513484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this IE is not valid and shall not be read.** [End 5GC002249-D]\*\*\*\* | 5G\_L2\_871 | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 [0…31] | 5GC002249-B |
| patternIdPolList | array[numOfPatternIdPol] [2*numOfXpolBeams] of u16,  the maximum size is 14*8. | DFE vector list of Pattern IDs for both polarization (XpolBeam). Even index is associated to +45° polarization and odd one to -45° polarization. Couple {+45°,-45°} is defined as one cross-polarized beam (XpolBeam). **[5GC002249-D] in ECPRI, in case of actEcpriPhase2 activated (5G\_L1\_IF\_20\_replaced([11512165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRnXwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_IF\_158\_replaced([11513484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this IE is not valid and shall not be read.** [End 5GC002249-D]\*\*\*\* | 5G\_L2\_871 | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** array[numOfPatternIdPol] [2*numOfXpolBeams] of u16,  the maximum size is 14*8 | 5GC001626-B |
| calibrationBitMap | u16 | **[Before CNI-86060] Bitmap (14 bits) that indicates the symbols is used for calibration in Radio Module note : only data part of the NR-slot used for calibration (10 or 11 symbols per TTI in 5G18A)** Bit : 1 when calibration is set, 0 when no calibration set **[CNI-86060] Bit : forced to 0, due to lack of support by all the RUs otherwise** [End CNI-86060]\*\*\*\* | 5G\_L2\_486 | **Loner/Loki/AiC/Thor:** u16 | CNI-86060 |

#### 2.2.5.1.2 SsBlock Send Request Message

###### 2.2.5.1.2.1 Loki/Thor/AiC/GPU

**2.2.5.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11512511`)

Loki/Thor/AiC/GPU
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_SsBlockSendReq message content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_SsBlockSendReqL1sw message content:**

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_SsBlockSendReq continues as** DlData\_SsBlockSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15507\_replaced([11512522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbEPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_SsBlockSendReq continues as** DlData\_SsBlockSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_69\_replaced([11512511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRp0B_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_SsBlockSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_SsBlockSendReqLoner or **DlData\_SsBlockSendReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*
* The origin of the parameters in this Table is L2-PS.
* There is no additional column in this table.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **L1 HW Support** | **First Feature** |
| subcellId | u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gvuZ8WGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). SubcellId is meant to be used as unrestricted ID and therefore L1 should accept any u8(exclude 0xFF) value. |  | **Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax]** **[End CB016075-K]** |  |

| enhTransScheme | u8 {Disabled = 0, EnhTransForNonBF = 1} | Indicates whether enhance precoding scheme is used for SSB transmission.   Applicable only in case CL/OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO mode with non-beamforming. Otherwise, set to default value 0 by L2PS. | **IF dlMimoMode = {0, 2, 4, 5}** **OR  “actBeamforming = True:** **NOT enhTransScheme = 1** | AiC:   **Loki:** u8 {Disabled = 0, EnhTransForNonBF = 1}   **Thor:** u8 {Disabled = 0, EnhTransForNonBF = 1} **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: u8 {Disabled = 0}** **[End CB016075-K]** | CB013440-A |
| activeSsBlocks | u8 | Bitmap indicating active (transmitted) SS Blocks which contain Synchronization Signals and PBCH. 1 means active (transmission) and 0 means no transmission of a SS Block. Most significant bit (MSB) is mapped to the first SS Block in time. For SCS = 15 kHz up to 1 bit can be set (MSB) For SCS = 30 kHz up to 2 bits can be set (MSB and MSB-1). For SCS = 240 kHz up to 4 bits can be set.   Examples: (SCS = 30 kHz) 0x80 - enables only the first SS Block 0x40 - enables only the second SS Block (SCS = 240 kHz) 0x90 - enables first and fourth (last possible) SS Block   See also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4114. | IF: “SCS” of SSB = 15kHz,   Not:“activeSsBlocks” & “0x70” != 0;     IF: “SCS” of SSB = 30kHz,   Not: “activeSsBlocks” & “0x30” != 0; | **Loki/AiC/Thor[CB016075-K]/GPU[End CB016075-K]: u8** |  |

| numCeAxcIndex | **[before 5GC002190-A]** u8 {2} **[End 5GC002190-A]**   **[5GC002190-A]** u8 {2 or 4} **[End 5GC002190-A]** **[CB012220-H]** u8 {1 or 2 or 4} **[End CB012220-H]** | Number of ceAxcIndex that are valid for this transmission request.   **[CB013440-A] Set to value 4 in case IE *enhTransScheme in \*DlData\_SsBlockSendReqL1sw message equals 1.****[End CB013440-A]*\* | **IF enhTransScheme =1** **NOT numCeAxcIndex !=4** | **Loki/AiC~~/Thor~~**:***\** \*Before 5G21B** u8 {2} **5G21B and onwards** u8 {2 or 4}   **Thor:** **[Before CB012220-H]** u8 {2 or 4} **[CB012220-H]** u8 {1 or 2 or 4} Value 1 is only used in A1 subcell type. **[End CB012220-H]** **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: u8 {2 or 4}** **[End CB016075-K]** | 5GC002190-A |

| patternId | array[4] of u16 | beam patternIds to be used for up to 4 transmissions of SSB, and the eCPRI control message generation. The upto 4 values allowed correspond to the ActiveSsBlocks (which allows upto 4 SS bursts supported per SSB send request message, that may use different beams). The patternIds will be used from the array of 4 based on the SSB position based on the activeSsBlocks bitmap. (e.g. if the bitmap is 0x40 corresponding to second SSB position only, then only the second position in patternId array is needed). |  | **Loki/AiC/Thor: array[4] of u16** **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: array[4] of u16** **[End CB016075-K]** | 5GC000399-K |

Most significant bit (MSB) is mapped to the first SS Block in time. For SCS = 15 kHz up to 1 bit can be set (MSB) For SCS = 30 kHz up to 2 bits can be set (MSB and MSB-1). | patternId | array[4] of u16 | beam patternIds to be used for up to 4 transmissions of SSB, and the eCPRI control message generation. (e.g. if the bitmap is 0x40 corresponding to second SSB position only, then only the second position in patternId array is needed). |  | **Loner: array[4] of u16** | 5GC000399-K |

| startDciIndex                                                                                                 | u8                                                                                                                                                                | startDciIndex which will only be used in eCPRI 7-2e.   startDciIndex denotes dciIndex of first DCI info in each DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw message.   [Before CB012733-SR-A] Currently: [End CB012733-SR-A] 1) if there is only one DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw for DL DCI so startDciIndex value in this message should be 0 when message is for DL DCI. 2) if there is only one DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw for UL DCI so startDciIndex value in this message should be 128 when message is for UL DCI.     [Before CB012733-SR-A] In future: [End CB012733-SR-A] 3) if there are more than one DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw messages for DL DCI then startDciIndex value of each message should be in range [0..127] and sum of this parameter startDciIndex and numOfDci should not be exceed 127. 4) if there are more than one DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw messages for UL DCI then startDciIndex value of each message should be in range [128..255] and sum of this parameter startDciIndex and numOfDci should not exceed 255. 5) L2PS should set startDciIndex sequentially like example below:   For example, there are multiple PDCCH messages for DL and UL: assume 3 PDCCH messages for DL DCI, 3 PDCCH message for UL DCI:   **1**st **PDCCH message for DL DCI (include 2 DL DCIs):*****\* startDciIndex = 0 dciInfo: numOfDci = 2* \*2**nd ***\**\*PDCCH message for DL DCI (include 5 DL DCIs)*****\**** *startDciIndex = 2 dciInfo: numOfDci = 5* *3**nd* ***\**PDCCH message for DL DCI (include 8 DL DCIs)*****\**** *startDciIndex = 7 dciInfo: numOfDci = 8* *4**rd* *PDCCH message for UL DCI (include 4 UL DCIs)****\** startDciIndex = 128 dciInfo: numOfDci = 4** 5**th** PDCCH message for UL DCI (suppose 5 UL DCIs)***\**\* startDciIndex = 132 dciInfo: numOfDci = 5** 6**th** PDCCH message for UL DCI (suppose 6 UL DCIs)**\***\* startDciIndex = 137 dciInfo: numOfDci = 6   [CB012733-SR-A] CB012733-SR-A will support up to 3 PDCCH symbols with (startSymbolNumber, numOfSymbols) of following (0,1) (1,1) (2,1) in DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw message for one subcell in one slot with following combinations and both L1 and L2 should handle this parameter startDciIndex as described above correctly:    1 DL, 1 UL,   1 DL + 1 UL, 2 DL, 2 UL,   3 DL, 3 UL, 2 DL + 1 UL, 1 DL + 2 UL.    Here "DL" means that there is one DL PDCCH occasion in this OFDM symbol, "UL" means that there is one UL PDCCH occasion in this OFDM symbol. "3DL" implies that there is one DL PDCCH occasion in each symbol and totally there are 3 OFDM symbols for DL. "3UL" implies that there is one UL PDCCH occasion in each symbol and totally there are 3 OFDM symbols for UL. "2 DL + 1 UL" implies that there is one DL PDCCH occasion in each symbol and totally there are 2 OFDM symbols for DL, and there is one UL PDCCH occasion in each symbol and totally there is 1 OFDM symbol for UL. "1 DL + 2 UL" implies that there is one DL PDCCH occasion in each symbol and totally there is 1 OFDM symbol for DL, and there is one UL PDCCH occasion in each symbol and totally there are 2 OFDM symbols for UL.     Note: CB012733-SR-A will not introduce L1-L2 IF change. [End CB012733-SR-A] Note: L2PS will fill this parameter startDciIndex no matter whether it is eCPRI 7-2e or not and on all HW platforms. L1 should only handle this parameter on Thor with eCPRI 7-2e and ignore it otherwise. | **Thor:** u8   **Loki/AiC: not supported** [CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] Odin:u8 [End CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: not supported [End CB016075-K]                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | CB009170-C            |

###### 2.2.5.2.2.1.2 Loner

**2.2.5.2.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11512575`)

Loner
**[CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_PdcchSendReqLoner message content:**

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_PdcchSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdcchSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15509\_replaced([11512575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbHPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_PdcchSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_74\_replaced([11512566](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_PdcchSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_PdcchSendReqLoner or **DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*
* The origin of the parameters in this Table is L2-PS.
* There is no additional column in this table.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **First Feature** |
| subcellId | u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gvuZ8WGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). For Loner, subcellId maximum value supported is 7 and subcellId numbering shall be at L1/L2 intance level. | **Loner:** u8 [0..7] |  |
| sfn | u16 [0..1023] | System Frame Number (38.211 §4.3.1 & 38.331 §6.2.2) | **Loner:** u16 [0..1023] |  |
| slot | u8 [0..79] | NR-slot (38.211 §4.3.2) | **Loner:** u8 [0..79] |  |
| beamId | u8 [0..63] | beamId on which the scheduled PDCCH is sent. NOTE: This information is for tracking only but not evaluated by L1. | **Loner:** u8 [0..63] |  |
| ~~msgCountCtrl~~ Not used. | Not used. | Not used. | Not used. |  |
| startDciIndex | u8 | startDciIndex which will only be used in eCPRI 7-2e.   startDciIndex denotes dciIndex of first DCI info in each DlData\_PdcchSendReq message.     Currently: 1) there is only one DlData\_PdcchSendReq for DL DCI so startDciIndex value in this message should be 0 when message is for DL DCI. 2) there is only one DlData\_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI so startDciIndex value in this message should be 128 when message is for UL DCI.     In future: 3) if there are more than one DlData\_PdcchSendReq messages for DL DCI then startDciIndex value of each message should be in range [0..127] and sum of this parameter startDciIndex and numOfDci should not be exceed 127. 4) if there are more than one DlData\_PdcchSendReq messages for UL DCI then startDciIndex value of each message should be in range [128..255] and sum of this parameter startDciIndex and numOfDci should not exceed 255. 5) L2PS should set startDciIndex sequentially like example below:   For example, there are multiple PDCCH messages for DL and UL: assume 3 PDCCH messages for DL DCI, 3 PDCCH message for UL DCI:   **1**st **PDCCH message for DL DCI (include 2 DL DCIs):*****\* startDciIndex = 0 dciInfo: numOfDci = 2* \*2**nd ***\**\*PDCCH message for DL DCI (include 5 DL DCIs)*****\**** *startDciIndex = 2 dciInfo: numOfDci = 5* *3**nd* ***\**PDCCH message for DL DCI (include 8 DL DCIs)*****\**** *startDciIndex = 7 dciInfo: numOfDci = 8* *4**rd* *PDCCH message for UL DCI (include 4 UL DCIs)****\** startDciIndex = 128 dciInfo: numOfDci = 4** 5**th** PDCCH message for UL DCI (suppose 5 UL DCIs)***\**\* startDciIndex = 132 dciInfo: numOfDci = 5** 6**th** PDCCH message for UL DCI (suppose 6 UL DCIs)**\***\* startDciIndex = 137 dciInfo: numOfDci = 6   Note: L2PS will fill this parameter startDciIndex no matter whether it is eCPRI 7-2e or not and on all HW platforms. L1 should only handle this parameter on Thor with eCPRI 7-2e and ignore it otherwise. | **Loner: not supported** |  |
| numOfDci | **[Before 5GC002537-A, 5GC002537-B] u8 [1..8]** **[End 5GC002537-A, 5GC002537-B]**   **[5GC002537-A, 5GC002537-B]** u8 [1..16] **[End 5GC002537-A, 5GC002537-B]** | See 5G\_L1\_2246   Note that this parameter does not exist explicitly, but instead can be obtained in MULTI implementation by dciInfo.length. | **Loner:** u8 [1..16] | 5GC000679-D |
| Per DCI: |  |  |  |  |
| >rnti | u16 | used for CRC parity bits scrambling  (38.212 §7.3.2 & 38.321 §7.1).   **NOTE:** **[5GC000733-F] P-RNTI** is used **[End 5GC000733-F]*****\** \*[5GC000742-A] SI-RNTI is used** [End 5GC000742-A]***\** \*[CB008124-B] C-RNTI or CS-RNTI for CG activation, CG deactivation and CG retransmission is used** [End CB008124-B]\*\*\*\* | **Loner:** u16 |  |
| >coresetConfigLoner | Structure, see separate definition in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15510\_replaced([11512597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCIPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | Structure with CORESET configuration.   **Note: this structure is for descriptive purpose only and its elements are directly inserted here in the implementation.** | **Loner:** 5G\_L1\_IF\_75\_replaced([11512588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbH_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  |
| >pdcchDmrsConfigLoner | Structure, see separate definition in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15512\_replaced([11512640](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCKvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | Structure with DMRS configuration.   **Note: this structure is for descriptive purpose only and its elements are directly inserted here in the implementation.** | **Loner:** 5G\_L1\_IF\_77\_replaced([11512632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  |
| >dciConfigLoner | Structure, see separate definition in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15513\_replaced([11512619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCJfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | Structure with DCI configuration.   **Note: this structure is for descriptive purpose only and its elements are directly inserted here in the implementation.** | **Loner:** 5G\_L1\_IF\_76\_replaced([11512609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  |

| >eCpriConfigLoner | Structure, see separate definition in  5G\_L1\_IF\_15573\_replaced([11512680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpMPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | Configuration structure for CPRI and eCPRI configuration purpose for given channel and slot.   **Note: this structure is for descriptive purpose only and its elements are directly inserted here in the implementation.** | **Loner:** 5G\_L1\_IF\_110\_replaced([11512672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCMvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  |
| >dciBitset | u8 | LSB **bit is the flag indicating if this DCI overlapped with PDSCH in time-frequency resource.** 0: no overlapping between DCI and PDSCH. 1: this DCI overlapped with PDSCH, PDSCH needs to rate match around this DCI.   By default, it is set to 0. | **Loner:** Not supported |  |
| >rachStatus | u8 enum { 0: OTHER, 2: MSG2, 3: MSG3, 4: MSG4, 5: MSG5 } | Indication of RACH message type which will be sent or received.   **Note: this field is used only for debugging purpose.** | **Loner:** u8 enum { 0: OTHER, 2: MSG2, 3: MSG3, 4: MSG4, 5: MSG5 }   Note: when CNI-82897 is developed, Loner is only target platform to use this parameter. But L2PS will send this parameter no matter whether it is Loner, Loki or Thor. Then it is found that Loki and Thor also use this parameter for debugging purpose. |  |

##### 2.2.5.2.2.3 DciConfig Struct

###### 2.2.5.2.2.3.0-1 DciConfig Struct Loki/Thor/AiC/Odin/GPU (ID: 11512606)

**2.2.5.2.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11512609`)

DciConfig Struct
**[Before CNI-132817]**

DciConfig:

**[CNI-132817]**

DciConfigL1sw:

Important note:

* The old **DciConfig struct is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**
* Into **DciConfigLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15513\_replaced([11512619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCJfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdcchSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15509\_replaced([11512575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbHPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*
* Into **DciConfigL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_76\_replaced([11512609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_74\_replaced([11512566](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

This structure is used in **[Before CNI-132817] DlData\_PdcchSendReq [CNI-132817] DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw [End CNI-132817] message.**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **First Feature** |
| >pdcchDciTransmitPower | s16 [-852...0] | PDCCH transmit power in relative dBFS by step of .1 dB. Its value is constant for a given channel bandwidth. see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2553. | **Loki/AiC/Thor:** s16 [-852...0] [CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] Odin: s16 [-852...0] [End CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: s16 [-852...0] [End CB016075-K] |  |
| >dciSize | u8 [12..140] | **NOTE: For more details about the supported DCI formats, please refer to L2-PS requirements 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4932, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4937, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4440, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10502** | **Loki/AiC/Thor:** u8 [12..140] [CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] Odin: u8 [12..140] [End CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: u8 [12..140] [End CB016075-K] |  |
| >dciPayload | array[18] of u8 | DCI payload. Padding bits (if any) are located on the least significant bits of the octet (u8). Bits in unused octets are set to 0. New formats to be supported are described in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_12960, 5G\_RAN\_UP\_6974, 5G\_RAN\_UP\_6977. | **Loki/AiC/Thor:** array[18] of u8 [CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] Odin: array[18] of u8 [End CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: array[18] of u8 [End CB016075-K] |  |
| >dciScramblingSequenceInit | u16 [0..65535] | **[PR559111]** Initialization of the Scrambling sequence for the data transmission. nID and nRNTI from the initialization formula in 5G\_UP\_IF\_645. See 38.211, section 7.3.2.3.   nID is equal to *dciScramblingSequenceInit*   nRNTI = *rnti if the value of this parameter within the range [1008..65535]. Otherwise, nRNTI =0.* When the 5G-L2-PS selects a common search space, this attribute is set to the physCellId. Otherwise, the ueSssDmrsScramblingId of the associated CORESET is used.   **[CB008124-B] nRNTI is calculated based on *dciScramblingRnti instead. \*\*[End CB008124-B]***[End PR559111]\*\*   For details, refer to 5G\_L1\_2266\_replaced([11441239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_fWEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_6359\_replaced([11441044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_eIAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loki/AiC/Thor:** u16 [0..65535] [CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] Odin:u16 [0..65535] [End CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: u16 [0..65535] [End CB016075-K] |  |
| >dciScramblingRnti | u16 [0..65535] | C-RNTI of the UE used to calculate nRNTI from the scrambling sequence initialization formula. See 38.211, section 7.3.2.3.   If value of *dciScramblingSequenceInit is within the range [1008..65535], nRNTI =* dciScramblingRnti.\*\* Otherwise, nRNTI  = 0.   For details, refer to 5G\_L1\_2266\_replaced([11441239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_fWEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_6359\_replaced([11441044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_eIAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loki:** u16 [0..65535]   **AiC: Not supported.**   **[CB009055-5G-A]** **Thor:** u16 [0..65535] (parity from CB008124) **[End CB009055-5G-A]** [CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] Odin:u16 [0..65535] [End CB012115-SR-GA, CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: Not supported [End CB016075-K] | CB008124-B |

**[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2** [End CNI-122313]\*\*\*\*

**[End CNI-132817]**

Important note:

* The old DciConfig struct is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.
* Into DciConfigLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15513\_replaced([11512619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCJfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in DlData\_PdcchSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15509\_replaced([11512575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbHPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message
* Into DciConfigL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_76\_replaced([11512609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in DlData\_PdcchSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_74\_replaced([11512566](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Description | L1 HW Support | First Feature |
| >pdcchDciTransmitPower | s16 [-852...0] | PDCCH transmit power in relative dBFS by step of .1 dB. Its value is constant for a given channel bandwidth. see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2553. | Loner: s16 [-852...0] |  |
| >dciSize | u8 [12..140] | NOTE: For more details about the supported DCI formats, please refer to L2-PS requirements 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4932, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4937, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4440, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10502 | Loner: u8 [12..140] |  |
| >dciPayload | array[18] of u8 | DCI payload. Padding bits (if any) are located on the least significant bits of the octet (u8). Bits in unused octets are set to 0. New formats to be supported are described in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_12960, 5G\_RAN\_UP\_6974, 5G\_RAN\_UP\_6977. | Loner: array[18] of u8 |  |
| >dciScramblingSequenceInit | u16 [0..65535] | Initialization of the Scrambling sequence for the data transmission. nID and nRNTI from the initialization formula in 5G\_UP\_IF\_645. See 38.211, section 7.3.2.3.   nID is equal to dciScramblingSequenceInit   nRNTI = rnti if the value of this parameter within the range [1008..65535]. Otherwise, nRNTI =0. When the 5G-L2-PS selects a common search space, this attribute is set to the physCellId. Otherwise, the ueSssDmrsScramblingId of the associated CORESET is used. nRNTI is calculated based on dciScramblingRnti instead.   For details, refer to 5G\_L1\_2266\_replaced([11441239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_fWEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_6359\_replaced([11441044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_eIAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | Loner: u16 [0..65535] |  |
| >dciScramblingRnti | u16 [0..65535] | C-RNTI of the UE used to calculate nRNTI from the scrambling sequence initialization formula. See 38.211, section 7.3.2.3.   If value of dciScramblingSequenceInit is within the range [1008..65535], nRNTI = dciScramblingRnti. Otherwise, nRNTI  = 0.   For details, refer to 5G\_L1\_2266\_replaced([11441239](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_fWEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_6359\_replaced([11441044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_eIAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | Loner: u16 [0..65535] | CB008124-B |

| [1] | valid combination of polarizationSelection/pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 and dlMimoMode. **[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2** [End CNI-122313]\*\*\*\*

### 2.2.5.3 Physical Downlink Shared Channel Send

#### 2.2.5.3.0-1 Physical Downlink Shared Channel Send Document Owner Hui Cheng (ID: 11512688)

#### 2.2.5.3.1 General

**2.2.5.3.1.0-5**  (ID: `11512723`)

General
For each DL Transport Block scheduled by 5G-L2-PS in a DL data subframe/NR-slot, 5G-L2-PS provides a DlData\_PdschSendReq message to 5G-L1-DL containing e.g. the range of OFDM symbols to be used, PRB allocation, transmission scheme and MCS.

**[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2** [End CNI-122313]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-GA] 5G-L1-DL (BB) shall support the requirements above in Odin.**[End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-GA]\*\*\*\*

[CB016075-K] 5G-L1-DL(BB) shall support the requirement above on GPU[End CB016075-K]

---

##### 2.2.5.3.1.1 Max number of DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one Transport Block

##### 2.2.5.3.1.1-1 Max number of DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one Transport Block

**2.2.5.3.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11512727`)

Max number of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one Transport Block
For each DL data packet scheduled by 5G-L2-PS in a range of OFDM symbols in a DL data subframe/NR-slot, 5G-L2-LO provides the payload to 5G-L1-DL:

* If the maximum PDSCH payload size is "9KB" (refers to 5G\_L1\_IF\_15400\_replaced([11512986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the max number of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one Transport Block:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Loner | Loki | Thor | Odin |
| The max number of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one TB | \* Two antenna ports: 9 \* Four antenna ports: 17 | \* One antenna ports: 5 \* Two antenna ports: 9 \* Four antenna ports: [Before CB008370-AA]17[CB008370-AA]18 [End CB008370-AA] | \* One antenna ports: 5 \* Two antenna ports: [Before CB008949-A] 9 [CB008949-A] 11 [End CB008949-A] \* Four antenna ports: [Before CB008949-A] [Before CB008370-AA] 17 [CB008370-AA] 18 [End CB008370-AA][CB008949-A] 22 [End CB008949-A] | **[CB012115-SR-IA]** \* Two antenna ports: 9 **[End CB012115-SR-IA]** **[CB012115-SR-IB, CB012115-SR-GA]** \* Four antenna ports: 17 **[End CB012115-SR-IB, CB012115-SR-GA]** |

[CB012979-H]

* If the maximum PDSCH payload size is "64KB" (refers to 5G\_L1\_IF\_15400\_replaced([11512986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the max number of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one Transport Block:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
|  | Thor |
| The max number of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one TB | - Case 1: PDSCH transport block is fragmented by 64KB only: \* One antenna ports: 1 \* Two antenna ports: 2 \* Four antenna ports: [Before CB008949-A] 3 [CB008949-A] 4 [End CB008949-A] - Case 2: PDSCH transport block is fragmented by both 64KB and 9KB, or fragmented by 9KB only: \* One antenna ports: 5 \* Two antenna ports: [Before CB008949-A] 9 [CB008949-A] 11 [End CB008949-A] \* Four antenna ports: [Before CB008949-A] 18 [CB008949-A] 22 [End CB008949-A] |

[End CB012979-H]

[CB016075-SR-F, **CB016066-C]**

If the maximum PDSCH payload size is "PAYLOAD\_SIZE\_340K " for GPU HW (refers to [11512986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the max number of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq messages per one Transport Block should be one.

[End CB016075-SR-F, **CB016066-C]**

Note: the maximum transport block size defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4621 exceeds the maximum payload size in L1-L2 interface (5G\_L1\_IF\_97\_replaced([11513002](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRtebfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This causes fragmentation of message into several fragments**.**

**[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2** [End CNI-122313]\*\*\*\*

---

#### 2.2.5.3.2 DlData_PdschSendReq message

##### 2.2.5.3.2.1 DlData_PdschSendReq message content

###### 2.2.5.3.2.1.0-1 DlData_PdschSendReq message content Loki/Thor/Odin/AiC/GPU (ID: 11512745)

**2.2.5.3.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11512751`)

DlData\_PdschSendReq message content
[Before CNI-132817]

DlData\_PdschSendReq message content:

[CNI-132817]

DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw message content:

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_PdschSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15515\_replaced([11512767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_PdschSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_PdschSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner or **DlData\_PdschSendReqReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*
* The origin of the parameters in this Table is L2-PS.
* There is no additional column in this table.

Default value is 0 and it means no dump is needed. - LSB bit 7: 0 means BWV and CE results are saved in snapshot history buffer (HB) file. 1 means BWV and CE results are saved in local HB file. - LSB bit 0~6: gives the beamforming (BF) subband granularity. For example, 3 means that every third BF subband reuqires BWV and CE dump. **[CB009527-D]** IE moved to *PdschRtBfConfig (5G\_L1\_IF\_15303\_replaced([11512951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteYPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as per UE grant level parameter* **[End CB009527-D]** | **[Before CB009527-D]** **Loki/AiC:** Not supported **Thor: u8** **[CB009527-D]** IE moved to *PdschRtBfConfig (5G\_L1\_IF\_15303\_replaced([11512951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteYPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as per UE grant level parameter* **[End CB009527-D]** |  | CB009527-C |

[End CB012971-C] See 5G\_L1\_4354\_replaced([11439285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_XaS_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loki/AiC/Thor/[CB012115-**SR-IA, CB012115-**SR-GA] Odin [End CB012115-**SR-IA, CB012115-**SR-GA]*****\****\*[CB016075-K]/GPU[End CB016075-K]: u8[1..16] |  |  |

###### 2.2.5.3.2.1.0-2 DlData_PdschSendReq message content Loner (ID: 11512761)

**2.2.5.3.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11512767`)

DlData\_PdschSendReq message content
[CNI-132817]

---

## DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner message content:

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_PdschSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15515\_replaced([11512767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_PdschSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_PdschSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner or **DlData\_PdschSendReqReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*
* The origin of the parameters in this Table is L2-PS.

## - There is no additional column in this table.

**2.2.5.3.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11512781`)

**[Before CNI-132817]**

**PdschSpatialConfig:**

**[CNI-132817]**

**PdschSpatialConfigL1sw:**

Important note:

* The old **PdschSpatialConfig struct is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**
* Into **PdschSpatialConfigLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15523\_replaced([11512790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRsQQfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15515\_replaced([11512767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*
* Into **PdschSpatialConfigL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_89\_replaced([11512781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

| >antPort | u16 | Antenna ports bitmap indicating used antenna port number(s). 1 means antenna port is used, 0 means unused. | Index | Invalid parameter combinations | Note |
| Example | IF: “parameterA” = “valueA”,        AND “parameterB” = “valueB”, NOT: “parameterC” = “valueC”; | If “parameterA” = “valueA” AND “parameterB” = “valueB”, “parameterC” should not be set to “valueC”. |
| [1] | IF: “dlMimoMode” = "CL 8x4 MIMO", NOT: “spatialMode” = "single antenna", "Tx div" or "open loop spatial multiplexing"; |  |
| [2] | IF: “dlMimoMode” = "CL 2x2 MIMO", NOT: “spatialMode” = "Tx div"; |  |
| [3] | IF: “dlMimoMode” = "OL 2x2 MIMO", NOT: “spatialMode” = "Tx div" or "closed loop spatial multiplexing"; |  |
| [4] | IF: “dlMimoMode” = "CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO", NOT: “spatialMode” = "Tx div"; |  |
| [5] | IF: “dlMimoMode” = "OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO", NOT: “spatialMode” = "Tx div" or "closed loop spatial multiplexing"; |  |
| [6] | For FDD FR1 IF: “numOfLayers” = 1, NOT: “antPort” = 1001, 1002 or 1003; |  |
| [7] | For TDD FR2 IF “numOfLayers” = 1, NOT: “antPort” = 1001, 1002 or 1003; |  |
| [8] | For FDD FR1 IF: “numOfLayers” = 2, NOT: “antPort” = {1002, 1003}; |  |
| [9] | For TDD FR2 IF: “numOfLayers” = 2, NOT: “antPort” = {1002, 1003}; |  |
| [10] | For FDD FR1 IF: “dlMimoMode” = “1x1 Single Antenna” NOT: “spatialMode” = “Tx div” or “closed loop spatial multiplexing” or “open loop spatial multiplexing” |  |

[End CNI-132817]

###### 2.2.5.3.2.4.0-2 PdschPrecodingConfig structure Loner (ID: 11512837)

**2.2.5.3.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11512840`)

PdschPrecodingConfig structure
**[CNI-132817]**

**PdschPrecodingConfigLoner:**

Important note:

* The old **PdschPrecodingConfig struct is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**
* Into **PdschPrecodingConfigLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15522\_replaced([11512840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRsQTPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15515\_replaced([11512767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*
* Into **PdschPrecodingConfigL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_92\_replaced([11512828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRsQSvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

| >codebookIndex | enum{     VAL\_0 = 0,     VAL\_1 = 1,     VAL\_2 = 2,     VAL\_3 = 3,     VAL\_255 = 255 } | Precoding matrix index to be used for precoding. Applicable only to 2 antenna ports transmission and ignored in case of Open Loop scheme and CL scheme with 4x4 MIMO, see 5G\_L1\_5094\_replaced([11433380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_J-5fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_5103\_replaced([11434463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_MbJPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value 255 means "not significant".   For supported values, see 5G\_L1\_2075\_replaced([11434237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_L0GPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner:** enum{     VAL\_0 = 0,     VAL\_1 = 1,     VAL\_2 = 2,     VAL\_3 = 3,     VAL\_255 = 255 } | Invalid combination [1]; Invalid combination [2]; | 5GC001716-A |
| >i1Codebook4AntPorts | array [3] of u8 | Subsequent elements of the array correspond to i1,1, i1,2 and i1,3 from ([11434463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_MbJPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 38.214, §5.2.2.2.1 Applicable only to 4 antenna ports transmission and ignored in case of OL scheme and CL scheme with 2x2 MIMO. When an element of the array is set to 255, it means not significant.    Extended range for i1,1, is 0..15 with additionnal value of dlMimoMode, cf. ([11435279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_NpRPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This parameter shall be ignored by L1 for precoding, no need of test vectors. Extended range for i1,2 is 0..7 with additionnal value of dlMimoMode, cf. ([11435279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_NpRPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This parameter shall be ignored by L1 for precoding, no need of test vectors. **[CB016028-A]** All elements are set to 255 by L2PS in case IE *closedLoop3gppCodebook =3 (EnhCtrlChannelTransPrecoding).* **[End CB016028-A]** | **Loner:** array [3] of u8 | Invalid combination [3]; Invalid combination [4]; Invalid combination [5]; Invalid combination [7]; Invalid combination [8]; Invalid combination [9]; | 5GC000605-M |
| >i2Codebook4AntPorts | u8 | i2 from ([11434463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_MbJPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 38.214, §5.2.2.2.1. Applicable only to 4 antenna ports transmission and ignored in case of OL scheme and CL scheme with 2x2 MIMO. Applicable to 8 antenna ports CSI-RS transmission when dlMimoMode 8x4 closed loop SU MIMO is enabled.   **[CB016028-A]** Set to 255 by L2PS in case IE *closedLoop3gppCodebook =3 (EnhCtrlChannelTransPrecoding).* **[End CB016028-A]** | **Loner:** u8 [0..3, 255] | Invalid combination [6]; Invalid combination [10]; | 5GC000605-M |
| >pdschPrecodingOption4x4 | enum { NoPortSelection = 0, PortSelectionUpToRank2 = 1, PortSelectionUpToRank4 = 2, PortSelectionUpToRank1 = 3, NoPortSelectionWcsirsPrecoding = 4, PortSelectionUpToRank2WcsirsPrecoding = 5, PortSelectionUpToRank4WcsirsPrecoding = 6} | This **parameter can be used also for Open Loopand extedended range (value 3 not Used)**   Without beamforming, which is actBeamforming=FALSE, value 0 is applied, therefore no port selection.   Only value 0 shall be indicated by L2 with additionnal value of dlMimoMode, cf. 5G\_L1\_5109\_replaced([11435279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_NpRPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner:** enum { NoPortSelection = 0, PortSelectionUpToRank2 = 1, PortSelectionUpToRank4 = 2, NoPortSelectionWcsirsPrecoding = 4, PortSelectionUpToRank2WcsirsPrecoding = 5, PortSelectionUpToRank4WcsirsPrecoding = 6} | Invalid combination [11]; | 5GC000605-M |
| >pdschBundleSize | **u16 [1..273]** | Bundle size in PRB. Value 4 is expected for open loop precoding operation for above and below 6 GHz. For the list of possible combinations of MCS and PRB allocations, please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20401. Please also note that starting from 5GC000425-S, MCS is not used in L1-DL encoder but is conveyed for debugging purposes. | Loner: u16 [1..273] | Invalid combination [4]; |  |
| >rbgSize | u8 [2..16] | Size of the RBG (besides the first and the last one)   Per 3GPP 38.214 Table 5.1.2.2.1-1, the suppoted values are 2, 4, 8 and 16.   See 5G\_L1\_4258\_replaced([11429959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_BcCvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details. | Loner: u8 {2, 4, 8, 16} | Invalid combination [5]; | 5GC000679-B |
| >rbgSizeFirst | u8 [1..16] | Size of the first RBG allocated to UE.   See 5G\_L1\_4258\_replaced([11429959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_BcCvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details. | Loner: u8 [1..16] | Invalid combination [5]; | 5GC000679-B |
| >rat0Bitmap | u32 | The bitmap to indicate the frequency domain resource allocation type 0. The RBGs shall be indexed in the order of increasing frequency and starting at the lowest frequency of the bandwidth part. The order of RBG bitmap is such that RBG 0 to RBG NRBG-1 are mapped from MSB to LSB. The RBG is allocated to the UE if the corresponding bit value in the bitmap is 1, otherwise the RBG is not allocated to the UE.   When resource allocation type 1 is used, all bits shall be set to 0.   See 5G\_L1\_4257\_replaced([11429901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_BcBPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_4258\_replaced([11429959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_BcCvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details. | Loner: u32, Bit31 to bit14 are used now, bit13 to bit0 are reserved. |  | 5GC000679-B |

Restricted parameter combinations for PdschAllocationConfig structure:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| >baseGraph | u8 {1, 2} | Base Graph number | Loner: u8 {1, 2} |  |  |

pdschUnscheduledAreaConfig
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**pdschUnscheduledAreaConfig:**

**[CNI-132817]**

**pdschUnscheduledAreaConfigL1sw**

Important note:

* The old **pdschUnscheduledAreaConfig struct is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**
* Into **pdschUnscheduledAreaConfigLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15517\_replaced([11512937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRs3YfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15515\_replaced([11512767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*
* Into **pdschUnscheduledAreaConfigL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15220\_replaced([11512929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRs3X_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

This structure is used in **[Before CNI-132817] DlData\_PdschSendReq [CNI-132817] DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw [End CNI-132817] message.**

Unscheduled area is the **smallest,** rectangular and **contiguous area which covers common part of PDSCH and other channels/signals**.***\****\*

Note: 7-2a eCPRI FH shall use this structure to know the area which PDSCH shall skip due to occupied by other channels/signals when generating FCP.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| >unscheduledAreaStartPrb | u16 [0..273] | The start PRB of the area which PDSCH shall skip due to occupied by other channels/signals.   By default, it is 0. | **AiC:** Not supported **Loki/Thor BB:** u16 [0..273] | Invalid combination [1]; | CB008370-AA |
| >unscheduledAreaNumOfPrb | u16 [0..273] | The number of PRBs of the area which PDSCH shall skip due to occupied by other channels/signals. By default, it is 0. | **AiC:** Not supported **Thor BB:** u16 [0..273] | Invalid combination [2]; | CB008370-AA |
| >unscheduledAreaStartSymbol | u8 [0..1] | The start symbol of the area which PDSCH shall skip due to occupied by other channels/signals.   By default, it is 0. | **AiC:** Not supported **Loki/Thor BB:** u8 [0..1] | Invalid combination [3]; | CB008370-A~~A~~ |
| >unscheduledAreaNumOfSymbols | u8 [0..2] | The number of symbol of the area which PDSCH shall skip due to occupied by other channels/signals.   By default, it is 0. | **AiC:** Not supported **Loki/Thor BB:** u8 [0..2] | Invalid combination [4]; | CB008370-A~~A~~ |

Other values are reserved. - LSB bits 0~11 are used to indicate the value of the unique identifier of current UE. Valid range is between 0 and [Before CB014315-A] 15 [CB014315-A] 67 [End CB014315-A] (maximum [Before CB014315-A] 16 [CB014315-A] 68 [End CB014315-A]UEs can support SB BF simultaneously).   Note: in case of non-RT BF or non-eCPRI 7-2e FH type, *rtBfUeIndex should be set to default value 0x0FFF and L1 shall check patternId field for beamforming (as value in MSB bits 0~3 is 0).*   Refer to 5G\_L1\_15310\_replaced([11468132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEEfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Thor:** u16 **Loki/AiC:** Not supported |  | CB009527-A |

| >bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands | u8 | Beam weight vector (BWV) dump granularity. When activated, the corresponding channel estimates (CE) are also downloaded via same granularity. - LSB bit 7: 0 means BWV and CE results are saved in snapshot history buffer (HB) file. 1 means BWV and CE results are saved in local HB file. - LSB bit 0~6: gives the beamforming (BF) subband granularity.  Value 0 means no dump is needed.  For example, 3 means that every third granted BF subband requires BWV and CE dump.  Note: in case of non-RT BF or non-eCPRI 7-2e FH type, *bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands should be set to value 0.* | **Thor:** u8 **Loki/AiC:** Not supported |  | CB009527-D |

###### 2.2.5.3.2.10.0-2 PdschRtBfConfig Loner (ID: 11512955)

PdschRtBfConfig
**[CNI-132817]**

**PdschRtBfConfigLoner:**

Important note:

* The old **PdschRtBfConfig struct is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**
* Into **PdschRtBfConfigLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15516\_replaced([11512958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteYvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15515\_replaced([11512767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*
* Into **PdschRtBfConfigL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15303\_replaced([11512951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteYPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** DlData\_PdschSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| >rtBfUeIndex | u16 | Unique identifier of the UE that activates SB BF**.**   - MSB bits 0~3 are used to define BF type. Value 0 means non RT BF, value 1 means RT SB BF. Other values are reserved. - LSB bits 0~11 are used to indicate the value of the unique identifier of current UE. Valid range is between 0 and 15 (maximum 16 UEs can support SB BF simultaneously).   Note: in case of non-RT BF or non-eCPRI 7-2e FH type, *rtBfUeIndex should be set to default value 0x0FFF and L1 shall check patternId field for beamforming (as value in MSB bits 0~3 is 0).*   Refer to 5G\_L1\_15310\_replaced([11468132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEEfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner:** Not supported |  |  |
| >eirpEnable | u8 | A flag indicating if EIRP coefficient computation (5G\_L1\_16395\_replaced([11468106](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndC_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated for current UE grant. Value 0 means disabled while value 1 means enabled.   Note: in case of non-RT BF or non-eCPRI 7-2e FH type, *eirpEnable should be set to default value 0.* | **Loner:** Not supported |  |  |
| >bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands | u8 | Beam weight vector (BWV) dump granularity. When activated, the corresponding channel estimates (CE) are also downloaded via same granularity. - LSB bit 7: 0 means BWV and CE results are saved in snapshot history buffer (HB) file. 1 means BWV and CE results are saved in local HB file. - LSB bit 0~6: gives the beamforming (BF) subband granularity. For example, 3 means that every third BF subband reuqires BWV and CE dump. Value 0 means no dump is needed.   Note: in case of non-RT BF or non-eCPRI 7-2e FH type, *bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands should be set to value 0.* | **Loner:** Not supported |  |  |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Index** | **Invalid combination** | **Note** |
|  |  |  |

**[End CNI-132817]**

---

StreamConfig

StreamConfig

StreamConfigL1sw

o numStreamIndex <-> numCeAxcIndex

o streamIndex <-> ceAxcIndex

**[End 5GC002538-A, 5GC002538-C]**

**[End 5GC002538-A, 5GC002538-C]**

#### 2.2.5.3.3 DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message

##### 2.2.5.3.3.0-1 DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message Maximum PDSCH payload size (ID: 11512986)

**2.2.5.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11512990`)

DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message
5G-L1-DL shall set maxPdschPayloadSize in DlData\_AddressResp message to indicate 5G-L2-PS the L1 supported maximum PDSCH payload size. The supported values of maxPdschPayloadSize are:

* 0: "9KB"

Considering the bytes used by headers, the maximum size of PDSCH payload is 8960 bytes which is computed as:

8960 = 9000 – 8 (BIP header size) – 8 (SW event header size) – 24 (header size of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message)

* 1: "64KB"

Considering the bytes used by headers, the maximum size of PDSCH payload is 63960 bytes which is computed as:

63960 = 64000 – 8 (BIP header size) – 8 (SW event header size) – 24 (header size of DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message, shall be multiple of 8 bytes)

[CB016075-F, **CB016066-C]**

* 2: "PAYLOAD\_SIZE\_340K "

This value is used with shared memory as transport layer to remove message fragmentation

The maximum size of PDSCH payload is 340736 bytes which is computed as:

max\_code\_rate \* 273PRB \* 12SC \* 8 (256QAM) \* 8 layer \* 13 symbols / 8 bit = max\_code\_rate\* 340 704B

ceil\_to\_64B\_word( max\_code\_rate\* 340 704B + 4B CRC) = 340736

[End CB016075-F, **CB016066-C]**

The maximum PDSCH payload size shall be same in all subcells in one L1 instance.

For Loner, Loki, Thor in Cloud product (RINLINE2) [CB012115-SR-IA] Odin [End CB012115-SR-IA]:

Only “9KB” maximum payload size is supported. 5G-L1-DL shall set maxPdschPayloadSize in DlData\_AddressResp message to 0 ("9KB").

For Thor in classical products (ABIP/ABIQ/ASOG/ASOH):

Both “9KB” and “64KB” maximum payload size are supported. 5G-L1-DL shall set maxPdschPayloadSize in DlData\_AddressResp message based on the value of L1 R&D parameter *rdMaxPdschPayloadSize (refer to 5G\_L1\_14466\_replaced([11445217](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_vNuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

[CB016075-F, **CB016066-C]**

For AI-RAN/GPU products:

PAYLOAD\_SIZE\_340K shall be used to remove fragmentation and utilize SHM memory based transport layer benefits

[End CB016075-F, **CB016066-C]**

---

##### 2.2.5.3.3.0-2 DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message content (ID: 11512994)

**2.2.5.3.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11512998`)

DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message
**Loki/Thor/Odin/AiC/GPU**

---

**2.2.5.3.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11513002`)

DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqL1sw message content:**

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15526\_replaced([11513011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_97\_replaced([11513002](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRtebfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqLoner or **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

5G-L1-DL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message in L1 Loki HW.

It is expected that the first bit in DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq.payload shall be N\*8 bytes away from the message start, N is an integer. For that extra padding bytes can be added in header. This requirement is valid also for ABIL.

*Rationale: The alignment to 8 bytes shall be ensured in order to enable use of HW accelerator DMA on 5G-L1-DL on Loki (ABIO board) to re-assemble received DL payload packet fragments to a single block. The DMA works on data blocks which are aligned to 64 bit addresses.*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **First Feature** |
| subcellId | u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gvuZ8WGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). SubcellId is meant to be used as unrestricted ID and therefore L1 should accept any u8(exclude 0xFF) value. | **Loki/AiC/Thor/[CB012115-**SR-IA, CB012115-**SR-GA] Odin [End CB012115-**SR-IA, CB012115-**SR-GA]*****\**** *[CB016075-K]/GPU[End CB016075-K]**:*\* u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] |  |

**2.2.5.3.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11513007`)

DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message
Loner

---

**2.2.5.3.3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11513011`)

DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message
**[CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqLoner message content:**

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15526\_replaced([11513011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq continues as** DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_97\_replaced([11513002](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRtebfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqLoner or **DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

5G-L1-DL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message in L1 Loki HW.

It is expected that the first bit in DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq.payload shall be N\*8 bytes away from the message start, N is an integer. For that extra padding bytes can be added in header. This requirement is valid also for ABIL.

*Rationale: The alignment to 8 bytes shall be ensured in order to enable use of HW accelerator DMA on 5G-L1-DL on Loki (ABIO board) to re-assemble received DL payload packet fragments to a single block. The DMA works on data blocks which are aligned to 64 bit addresses.*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **First Feature** |
| subcellId | u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gvuZ8WGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). For Loner, subcellId maximum value supported is 7 and subcellId numbering shall be at L1/L2 intance level. | **Loner:** u8 [0..7] |  |
| sfn | u16 [0..1023] | System Frame Number (38.211 §4.3.1 & 38.331 §6.2.2) | **Loner:** u16 [0..1023] |  |
| slot | u8 [0..79] | NR-slot (38.211 §4.3.2) | **Loner:** u8 [0..79] |  |
| rnti | u16 | RNTI of UE. Used only for debugging purposes - ignored by L1. | **Loner:** u16 |  |
| tbIndex | u32 | Index of the transport block as specified in the message DlData\_PdschSendReq of the ongoing procedure. | **Loner:** u32 |  |

| ~~tbFragmentSize\_bytes~~ | ~~u32~~ | ~~Size of the current fragment in bytes~~ | ~~Loner:~~ ~~u32~~ |  |
| payload | "9KB": dynamic array[8960] of u8 "64KB": dynamic array[63960] of u8 | Payload of PDSCH Transport Block (or fragment). The payload size is variable.   The header size must be multiple of 8 bytes. For that extra padding bytes can be added.     The supported maximum paylod size is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15400\_replaced([11512986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).   The set of transmitted bytes is exactly tbFragmentSize\_bytes. Bits are serialized in the "payload" buffer as specified in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14741\_replaced([11516557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSEq1vvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner:** array[8960] of u8 |  |

**[End CNI-132817]**

---

###### 2.2.5.4.2.1.0-2 CSI-RS Send Request Message Content Loner (ID: 11513068)

**2.2.5.4.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11513072`)

CSI-RS Send Request Message Content
**[CNI-132817]**

**DlData\_CsiRsSendReqLoner message content:**

Important Note:

* On Loner platforms, **DlData\_CsiRsSendReq continues as** DlData\_CsiRsSendReqLoner (see [11513072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFevvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and on all other platforms, **DlData\_CsiRsSendReq continues as** DlData\_CsiRsSendReqL1sw (see [11513061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuFePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***\****\*
* Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **DlData\_CsiRsSendReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** DlData\_CsiRsSendReqLoner or **DlData\_CsiRsSendReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*
* The origin of the parameters in this Table are identified in the column “Parameter Origin”.
* There is an additional column, called parameter origin, in only those messages with a mix of origins.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **Parameter Origin** | **First Feature** |
| subcellId | u8 [0..dlSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). dlSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gvuZ8WGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). For Loner, subcellId maximum value supported is 7 and subcellId numbering shall be at L1/L2 intance level. | **Loner:** u8 [0..7] |  | L2-PS |  |

| numOfCsiResources | u8 [1...24] | Number of CSI-RS resources for a given slot. The maximum value is 10 symbol *2 = 20 CSI-RS resouces in a given slot(Slot type 41), where 10 means at most 10 symbols can be used for CSI-RS transmission in one slot, 2 means one C4 subcell can handle 2 CSI-RS resources simultaneously. The supported number is 2*6 CSI-RS for tracking and 4 CSI-RS for channel acquisition, totally 16 CSI-RS resources.     From 23R1 and onwards, the maximum value is 12 symbol *2 = 24 CSI-RS resouces in a given slot, where 12 means at most 12 symbols can be used for CSI-RS transmission in one slot, 2 means one C4 subcell can handle 2 CSI-RS resources simultaneously. The supported number is 2*6 CSI-RS for tracking and 2\*6 CSI-RS for channel acquisition, totally 24 CSI-RS resources   Note that this parameter does not exist explicitly, but instead can be obtained in MULTI implementation by csiRsResources.length.   For supported values, refer to [11444709](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_sxePvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). | **Loner:** u8 [1...20] | Invalid combination [1]; | L2-PS |  |

| [1] | The valid combination for antStream: IF "actBeamforming' ="True", THEN "antStream" = "0x3"; ELSE IF "dlMimoMode"="0" or "2", THEN "antStream"="0x3"; ELSE IF "dlMimoMode"="1" or "3", THEN "antStream"="0xF". |  | [12723272: 5G-L1-DL (BB) shall validate that antStream is equal to 0x3 in case DlData\_RimRsSendReq was received for subcell with "actBeamforming' ="True" configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwXgG4VEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/117) [12723276: 5G-L1-DL (BB) shall validate that antStream is equal to 0x3 in case DlData\_RimRsSendReq was received for subcell with "dlMimoMode"="0" or "2" configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_g1vpIG4WEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/117) [12723277: 5G-L1-DL (BB) shall validate that antStream is equal to 0xF in case DlData\_RimRsSendReq was received for subcell with "dlMimoMode"="0" or "2" configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mniBkG4WEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/117) |

The RBGs shall be indexed in the order of increasing frequency and starting at the lowest frequency of the bandwidth part. The order of RBG bitmap is such that RBG 0 to RBG NRBG-1 are mapped from MSB to LSB. Other values are reserved. - LSB bits 0~11 are used to indicate the value of the unique identifier of current UE. Valid range is between 0 and 15(maximum 16 UEs can support SB BF simultaneously).   Note: Here MSB bits should be 1 indicating RT SB BF.    Refer to 5G\_L1\_15310\_replaced([11468132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEEfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Thor: u16**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported** |  | CB012971-C |

| >>bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands | u8 | Beam weight vector (BWV) dump granularity. When activated, the corresponding channel estimates (CE) are also downloaded via same granularity. - LSB bit 7: 0 means BWV and CE results are saved in snapshot history buffer (HB) file. 1 means BWV and CE results are saved in local HB file. - LSB bit 0~6: gives the beamforming (BF) subband granularity.  Value 0 means no dump is needed. For example, 3 means that every third granted BF subband requires BWV and CE dump. | **Thor: u8**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported** |  | CB012971-C |
