## 2.2.6 DL logging Procedures

### 2.2.6.0-1 DL logging Procedures Document Owner Tao-Kerry Huang (ID: 11513189)

### 2.2.6.1 L2 buffer freeze indicate for L1 suspicious events

**2.2.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `11513196`)

L2 buffer freeze indicate for L1 suspicious events
Messages:

DlData\_DiagnosticInd

Purpose:

L1 informs L2 to freezes it's buffers.

Precondition:

L1 starts the collection and stores IQ data on BTS storage after NR L1 Event Triggered.

Addressing:

The message is sent to the L2 address which is got in the phase of DL address navigation.

For the L2 address, L2 should not create one new address. L2 should using the existing address which is one of the PDSCH/PDCCH response address.

Description:

[CNI-76719] L1 informs L2 immediately about the event trigger:

For IQ data capture, when L1 suspicious event is triggered and before L1 indicate OAM for BTS Snapshot. L1 informs L2 immediately by sending DlData\_DiagnosticInd (for DL Loki) to L2. L2 shall freeze L2 trace buffers after receiving this message [END CNI-76719].

Expected Exceptions:

Synchronized L2 Traces and L1 IQ sample collection

DlData\_DiagnosticInd message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Field Name | Format | Range | Description | First Feature |
| indType | UINT\_8 | { 0: Freeze ,   } | Indicate message purpose and origin | CNI-76719 |

---

### 2.2.6.2 Downlink Fast Antenna snapshot Request

**2.2.6.2.0-5**  (ID: `11513221`)

Downlink Fast Antenna snapshot Request
**DlData\_FastAntennaSnapshotResp message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Field Name | Format | Range | Definition | **First Feature** |
| status | UINT\_8 | **[Before CNI-82417]{ 0:NoError** 20: DefaultError } **[CNI-82417]** { 0:NoError 3:OutOfSequence 4:ServiceBusy [PR840468] ~~5:MissingMemory~~ [End PR840468] 6:DataNotAvailable 7:MinTimeRejection [PR840468] ~~8:RxUnderflow~~ ~~9:HwError~~ ~~10:DMAError~~ ~~11:FileError~~ ~~12:HaltOnResourcesLimit~~ [End PR840468] 13:SubcellNotConfigured 20:DefaultError } **[End CNI-82417]** | Positive / negative acknowledgment Refer to BTSC\_L1\_Req\_4892 for the details. | CNI-51355 **CNI-82417-A** |

[Before PR840468]

On reception of this message with positive acknowledgement (status=0: NoError),  L2 component shall increment an internal counter associated to request of this abnormal event.

if L1 response is not OK , L2 shall wait for a while e.g. 120 seconds before triggering next abnormal event. For these unsuccessful cases detailled to be add at CP3.

[PR840468]

if L1 response status = 0 indicate NoError, L2 shall increment an internal counter assoiated to request of this abnormal event.

if L1 response status = 4, 7 indicate busy status, L2 shall set a wait timer before triggering next abnormal event.

if L1 response status = 3, 6, 13, 20 indicate configration error, L2 shall not set a wait timer.

[End PR840468]

Above requirement shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW

**[CB009028-5G-A] Parity from CNI-82417:**

This requirement shall be supported for Thor**.**

**[End CB009028-5G-A]**

Downlink Message TX timestamping
12705476:
Downlink Message TX timestamping
12705476:
Downlink Message TX timestamping
12705476:
Downlink Message TX timestamping
12705476:
Downlink Message TX timestamping
TX timestamping mechanism:

* Transmitter shall set TX timestamp into the 24-bit timestamp field in SW event header
* When using this mechanism, the 24-bit timestamp is always in little endian.
* Platform SW (DU, vDU, L1) shall provide APIs to Transmitter and Receiver to write/read TX timestamp.
* Transmitter shall convert BCN into 24-bit timestamp (see mapping diagram below).  
  Here BCN is the secondary BCN in Classical BTS and common BCN in Cloud BTS.

Note: Platform SW API design and behavior will be specified in platform specifications.

For SW event header please refer to chapter 9.2 of Transport layer Architecture Specification, see: [12739382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CVIi0nkUEfCdZt6bzaG3fw)

BCN to Timestamp mapping diagram:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the structure of an "EM SW event header". The header is depicted as a series of bit fields, with the most significant bit (MSB) on the left and the least significant bit (LSB) on the right. The diagram shows two main components: "Timestamp" and "BCN".
The "EM SW event header" is described as being in "Big endian / network byte order".
The "Timestamp" is shown as a 24-bit field, further divided into two parts: a 10-bit section and a 14-bit section. The bits are numbered from 23 down to 0. There's an arrow indicating that the "Timestamp (in local machine endian)" is "Set in Little Endian".
Below the "Timestamp", the "BCN" (presumably a Base Clock Number or similar identifier) is shown as a larger field, spanning 63 bits down to 0. This field is divided into two parts: "N1 (40 bits)" and "N2 (24 bits)". The "N1" section is further subdivided into two parts, indicated by bit numbers 34-33 and 24-23. The "N2" section is subdivided into two parts, indicated by bit numbers 10-9 and 0.
There are also fields labeled "Reserved (8 bits)" and "Flags (8 bits)" at the top, and "Message type number (16 bits)" at the top right, all contributing to the overall header structure. The diagram uses colored blocks (light green for Timestamp, pink for N1, and yellow for N2) to visually represent these fields.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-07151037.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**[CB012115-IA]  Above requirement shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW** [End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a timing diagram illustrating the downlink (DL) scheduling and transmission windows in a 5G system. The diagram shows the timeline of events and their relationships.
Here's a breakdown of the elements:
\* **BCN = 0**: This indicates the beginning of a BCN (Broadcast Control Network) cycle, likely representing a time reference.
\* **frameStart (for SFN = 0)**: This marks the start of a frame, with SFN (System Frame Number) being 0.
\* **5G-L2-PS DL Scheduling and 5G-L2-LO**: This section represents the DL scheduling and L2 (Layer 2) control functions.
\* **5: DL Req TX window**: This is a time window for transmitting DL requests.
\* **T56\_Min**: This denotes a minimum time value, likely a delay or offset.
\* **5G-L1-DL (BB)**: This refers to the Layer 1 (Physical Layer) DL functions, specifically for the Baseband (BB).
\* **6: DL Req RX window**: This is a time window for receiving DL requests.
\* **Scheduling Start offset**: This indicates an offset from the frame start where scheduling begins.
\* **1**: This is a numbered event marker.
\* **A, B**: These are points in time or durations related to the scheduling.
\* **T56\_Max**: This denotes a maximum time value, likely a delay or offset.
\* **T\_BBToAnt**: This represents the time taken for the Baseband to transmit to the antenna.
\* **B' = B - T56\_Max**: This is a calculated time point derived from B and T56\_Max.
\* **A' = A - T56\_Min**: This is a calculated time point derived from A and T56\_Min.
\* **Rd**: This is a marker, possibly indicating a read or reception point.
\* **DL Slot**: This represents a downlink slot, which is a unit of time for data transmission.
The diagram visually depicts how the DL Req TX window and DL Req RX window are positioned relative to the frame start and scheduling start offset, with constraints defined by T56\_Min and T56\_Max. The calculated points A' and B' suggest specific timing requirements for the DL Req RX window based on the DL Req TX window and these time constraints. The T\_BBToAnt duration is also shown, indicating the time from baseband processing to antenna transmission. The DL Slot is shown as a period of time where data is transmitted.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-07221446.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

### 2.2.7.2 Non-Mixed FH Mode

#### 2.2.7.2.1 DL Timing Concept

**2.2.7.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11513234`)

DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept

DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:

11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
11513234:
DL Timing Concept
**DL Timings:**

5G-L1-DL expects to receive send request message every slot in which given channel/signal is supposed to be transmitted.

5G-L1-DL expects to receive send request message at the soonest (A + *T\_BB1ToAnt) us and at the latest (B +* T\_BB1ToAnt) us before DL NR-slot boundary.\*\*

Definition of **T\_BB1ToAnt:**

Total downlink delay from FH egress port to air interface time reference point.

May includes margin and SM buffering delay which is calculated by OAM.

Value of **T\_BB1ToAnt will be configured by OAM->L1 and OAM->CPRT->L2RT**, mapping to the parameters as below:\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **T\_BB1ToAnt** | **L1** | **L2RT** |
| CPRI (Loner) | =  **dlFiberLengthCompensationOffset (common) in API\_L1SW\_CPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG** | = **oneWayHWDelayDl** in PsCell\_CellSetupReq |
| CPRI/OBSAI  (Loki/Thor) | = **pathDelay  (of downlink channel) in API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_AXC\_REQ\_MSG** |  |
| eCPRI 7-2a (Loner) | = **tDlAdvanceUp (common) in API\_L1SW\_eCPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG** |  |
| eCPRI 7-2a (Loki/Thor) | = **tDlAdvanceUp of downlink channel PDXCH (EPhyChannelType\_Pdxch) in API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSG** |  |
| eCPRI 7-2e (Loki/Thor) | = **tDlAdvanceUp of downlink channel PDXCH (EPhyChannelType\_Pdxch72e) in API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSG** | = **oneWayHWDelayDl + 500us** In PsCell\_CellSetupReq |

Values of A and B are specified in the following requirements:

* For TDD FR1: 5G\_L1\_IF\_124\_replaced([11513242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTm_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For TDD FR2: 5G\_L1\_IF\_125\_replaced([11513254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTnvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For FDD: 5G\_L1\_IF\_126\_replaced([11513266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTofvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB013338-A]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with the exception of a light gray rectangular box in the bottom right corner. Inside this box, the text "DL channel/ signal" is written in black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_254.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB013338-A]

###### 2.2.7.2.2.1.2 eCPRI 7-2e

**2.2.7.2.2.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `12636368`)

eCPRI 7-2e
**DL Timings for TDD FR1 (eCPRI 7-2e):**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Message | Transmission Window |  | Reception Window |  |
| A [us] | B [us] | A’ [us] | B’ [us] |  |
| DlData\_SlotTypeReq | [Before CB013338-A] 3500 [CB013338-A] 3550 [End CB013338-A] | [Before CB013338-A] 0 [CB013338-A] 20 [End CB013338-A] | [CB013338-A] A - T56\_Min [End CB013338-A] | [CB013338-A] B - T56\_Max [End CB013338-A] |
| DlData\_CsiRsSendReq |  |  |  |  |
| DlData\_SsBlockSendReq |  |  |  |  |
| DlData\_PdcchSendReq |  |  |  |  |
| DlData\_PdschSendReq |  |  |  |  |
| DlData\_RimRsSendReq |  |  |  |  |
| [CB012971-C] DlData\_UePairingReq [End CB012971-C] |  |  |  |  |
| DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq | [Before CB013338-A] 3500 [CB013338-A] 3550 [End CB013338-A] | [Before CB013338-A] -200 [CB013338-A] -180 [End CB013338-A] |  |  |
| DlData\_PatternConfigReq | N/A |  |  |  |

With eCPRI 7-2e, it needs to reduce the advance of whole L2-L1 window with respect to FH egress port by 500us, to prevent HARQ performance degradation from larger T1a\_max\_up.

With eCPRI 7-2e, the value of A or B could be 0 or negative, L1 processing time is covered by enlarged downlink UP/FCP TX window.

With eCPRI 7-2e, OAM may configure oneWayHWDelayDl = T1a\_max\_up - 500 to L2-PS and TdlAdvanceUP = T1a\_max\_up to L1, L2-PS shall adapt to the real T1a\_max\_up to keep the L2-L1 window aligned between L2-PS and L1. Please refer to 5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level for the behavior of L2-PS.

[CB013338-A]  
Note\*: for definition of T56\_Min and T56\_Max, please refer to [12698062: L2->L1 transportation delay definition](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B6s3QlyREfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).  
[End CB013338-A]

[CB012115-GA] Above requirement shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW [End CB012115-GA]

### 2.2.7.3 Mixed FH mode

#### 2.2.7.3.0-1 Mixed FH mode Mixed Fronthaul mode is the mode which support CPRI and eCPRI FH modes in the same BB cell set. For the L1 mixed FH mode shall be understand as no separation between CPRI and eCPRI for subpool configuration in L1SW configuration message. (ID: 12577777)

#### 2.2.7.3.1 DL Timings

**2.2.7.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `12577782`)

DL Timings

12577782:
DL Timings
12577782:
DL Timings
12577782:
DL Timings
The requirements below are valid only for the Mixed FH Mode which mean fronthaulMode in the L1Config\_SwConfigurationReq is set to CPRI\_and\_eCPRI\_WMP\_ORAN.

5G-L1-DL expects to receive send request message every slot in which given channel/signal is supposed to be transmitted.

5G-L1-DL expects to receive send request message at the soonest T6aMax us and at the latest T6aMin us before DL NR-slot boundary.

Definition of T6aMax/T6aMin:

T6aMin  - Latest reception time of DL Req RX window for CPRI and eCPRI for DlData\_xSendReq messages which include L1 processing time and total downlink delay from FH egress port to air interface time reference point (may includes margin and SM buffering delay which is calculated by OAM).

T6aMax - Earliest reception time of DL Req RX window for CPRI and eCPRI for DlData\_xSendReq messages which include T6aMin and timing window for DL Req RX window.

Value of **T6aMin shall be configured by OAM->L1  and sent by L1Config interface for L1:**

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **T6aMin** | fronthaulMode (DlCell\_SetupReq) | **L1** |
|  | CPRI (Thor) | = t**6aMin  in [L1Config\_SetL1TimingReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0E-fQHi4EfCdZt6bzaG3fw)** |
| eCPRI 7-2a (Thor) | = t**6aMin**in [L1Config\_SetL1TimingReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0E-fQHi4EfCdZt6bzaG3fw)\*\*\*\* |  |

Value of T6aMax shall be calculated by L1 as sum of T6aMin + timing window for DL Req RX window.

Values of timing window for DL Req RX window are specified in the following requirement:

* For FDD: [12577979: FDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JzpO0DCyEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the timing of downlink (DL) transmissions in a 5G network. The diagram depicts events and time windows related to DL scheduling and reception.
**Key elements and their descriptions:**
\* **BCN = 0:** This indicates the beginning of a broadcast control channel (BCN) or a reference point in time, set to 0.
\* **frameStart (for SFN = 0):** This marks the start of a frame, specifically for a System Frame Number (SFN) of 0.
\* **5G-L2-PS DL Scheduling and 5G-L2-LO:** This represents a process or entity responsible for DL scheduling at Layer 2 (L2) in the Packet Switched (PS) domain and Layer 2 in the Logical Object (LO) domain.
\* **5: DL Req TX window:** This signifies a transmission window for a "DL Request" at some point in the process, labeled as step 5. The window is defined by a start and end time.
\* **5G-L1-DL (BB):** This represents the Physical Layer (L1) for downlink (DL) in the Baseband (BB) processing.
\* **6: DL Req RX window:** This signifies a reception window for a "DL Request" at some point in the process, labeled as step 6. This window is also defined by a start and end time.
\* **DL Slot:** This is a designated time slot for downlink data transmission.
\* **Vertical Lines:**
\* The leftmost vertical line represents the start of the sequence (BCN=0).
\* A dashed vertical line indicates a reference point in time.
\* A solid black vertical line labeled "Rd" likely represents a reception point or a synchronization event.
\* A solid green vertical line labeled "1" indicates a specific event or synchronization point.
\* **Horizontal Dashed Arrows:** These indicate the duration of time windows or the flow of time between events.
\* **Time Labels:**
\* **T56\_Min:** Minimum time difference between the start of the TX window (5) and the start of the RX window (6).
\* **T56\_Max:** Maximum time difference between the start of the TX window (5) and the start of the RX window (6).
\* **T5a\_Min:** Minimum time difference between the frame start and the start of the DL Slot.
\* **T5a\_Max:** Maximum time difference between the frame start and the start of the DL Slot.
\* **T6a\_Min:** Minimum time difference between the start of the RX window (6) and the start of the DL Slot.
\* **T6a\_Max:** Maximum time difference between the start of the RX window (6) and the start of the DL Slot.
The diagram illustrates that the DL Req TX window (5) and DL Req RX window (6) are defined relative to each other and to the overall frame structure. The DL Slot is scheduled within these constraints, with minimum and maximum timing requirements (T5a, T6a) from reference points.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-08061003.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 2.2.7.3.3 Timing validation of downlink request messages

**2.2.7.3.3.0-1**  (ID: `13465441`)

Timing validation of downlink request messages
L1 shall validate the downlink request messages are received within RX window.

Note:  Method is described as below for SW reference

For PDCCH/PDSCH/SSB/CSI-RS:

0 < T\_pkt  + N1/N2OffsetTa6MinIncluded - T\_rcv  < T\_winsize

For PDSCH payload:

0 < T\_pkt  + N1/N2OffsetTa6MinIncluded - T\_rcv + 200 < T\_winsize'

Parameters in above formula:

T\_pkt – Air interface time carried in message, indicating when the message shall be sent on air.

T\_rcv  - L2-L1 message receiving timing, represented by L1 local BCN.

N1/N2OffsetTa6MinIncluded  - parameters sent by L1 FH  to L1 PHY, an intermediate timing offset used to calculate BCN timing at L2-L1

message RX window close for the data, refer to [13428876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BB_7QByMEfGw_-Y2PB9B3w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

T\_winsize - L2-L1 rx window size for PDCCH/PDSCH/SSB/CSI-RS, shall be calculated from timing table: [12577980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JzpO0TCyEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) , e.g.,  T\_winsize = T6a(max) - T6a(min) (of PDCCH)

T\_winsize’ - L2-L1 rx window size for PDSCH payload, shall be calculated from timing table: [12577980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JzpO0TCyEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), e.g., T\_winsize' = T6a(max) - T6a(min) (of PDSCH payload)

---

#### 2.2.7.3.4 DLPHY internal processing timing management

**2.2.7.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `13465443`)

DLPHY internal processing timing management
13465443:
DLPHY internal processing timing management
In mixed-FH mode, L1 shall start internal data processing with reference to L2-L1 window close boundary.

Note: DLPHY shall manage the timing for all kinds of its data processing(like the job start of PENC, LENC, DSYM..) diagram below is for reference only.

Note: For CPRI case, DLFE job shall be start accurately with an advance to RP1 reference to avoid TD IQ buffer overflow or underflow, so either SW shall get CPRI RP1i information or calculate timing based on RP6 with assumption T\_L1\_processing\_DL\_CPRI = 750us according to [12532989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_83qDwBwcEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a timing diagram illustrating a downlink data flow. The diagram depicts various jobs and delays involved in processing and transmitting data.
Here's a breakdown of the elements:
**Key Timings and Boundaries:**
\* **tDL = 0 (OTA Time):** This marks the reference point for Over-The-Air time.
\* **Latest message receiving boundary at RP6:** This indicates a critical point for message reception.
**Jobs and Windows:**
\* **PENC Job:** A job that occurs after a window of size `T_winsize`.
\* **Downlink L2-L1 Window (pdcch):** A window for the PDCCH (Physical Downlink Control Channel) data.
\* **DSYM Job:** A job that follows the PENC Job after a "SW defined Delay".
\* **LENC Job:** A job that occurs after a window of size `T_winsize'`.
\* **Downlink L2-L1 Window (pdsch payload):** A window for the PDSCH (Physical Downlink Shared Channel) payload.
\* **DLFE Job:** A job that follows a "SW defined Delay" after the PDSCH payload window, and also after a "Fxied Delay".
**Delays:**
\* **T\_winsize:** The size of the first window.
\* **T\_winsize':** The size of the second window.
\* **SW defined Delay:** A delay that is defined by software, occurring after the PDCCH window and before the DSYM Job, and also after the PDSCH payload window and before the DLFE Job.
\* **Fxied Delay:** A fixed delay that occurs before the DLFE Job.
\* **71us:** A specific delay of 71 microseconds.
\* **T\_L1\_processing\_DL\_CPRI:** The processing time for L1 in the downlink over CPRI.
\* **T\_L1\_processing\_DL\_eCPRI:** The processing time for L1 in the downlink over eCPRI.
\* **pathDelayDL:** The downlink path delay.
\* **tDIAdvanceUp:** An advance time for uplink.
\* **t6amin:** A minimum time value.
**Other Elements:**
\* **CPRI RP1i:** Indicates a CPRI interface at RP1i.
\* Vertical dashed lines represent time progression.
\* Horizontal arrows indicate the duration of windows or the flow of time between events.
\* A red dashed vertical line represents the OTA Time reference.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04151740.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---
